	name = xxxx_Loc
	text = {
		localization_key = xxx_1
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = EU_parliament_Supermajority
	text = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_global_flag = european_constitution
				has_global_flag = european_federation
			}
		}
		localization_key = EU_parliament_Supermajority_loc_key
	}
}

### PG Western_Autocracy support ###
defined_text = {
	name = EU_parl_PG_wes_aut_support
	text = {
		trigger = {
			any_of_scopes = {
				array = global.EU_member
				has_global_flag = PG_wes_aut_support
			}
		}
		localization_key = EU_parl_PG_wes_aut_support_loc_key
	}
}
